This file contains a list of autonomous system numbers and names of all
registered ASNs.  The column on the right below contains the ARIN
database "handle" of the coordinator for the ASN.  White-pages
information may be obtained about any of the ASN coodinators in this
list querying the ARIN WHOIS server.  For questions or updates on this
information please contact the ARIN Registration Services Hostmaster staff,
HOSTMASTER@ARIN.NET.
